**Phase 91 — Complete.** All 199 test modules green. Sovereign GK Quantile Sketch (Greenwald–Khanna, 2001) — streaming **ε-approximate quantiles** (p50/p95/p99) over an unbounded stream in `O((1/ε)·log(εn))` space, with a hard guarantee: the value returned for a quantile `φ` has true rank within `±⌈εn⌉` of the requested rank. The summary is a value-sorted list of tuples `(v, g, Δ)` where `g = r_min(v_i) − r_min(v_{i−1})` (so `r_min(v_i) = Σ g_j`) and `Δ = r_max(v_i) − r_min(v_i)`; the invariant `g_i + Δ_i ≤ ⌊2εn⌋` is what bounds the error. **Insert** places `v` in sorted order with `g = 1`, `Δ = ⌊2εn⌋` (new min/max get `Δ = 0` — exact extremes). **Compress** (every `⌊1/2ε⌋` inserts) merges an adjacent pair when `g_i + g_{i+1} + Δ_{i+1} ≤ ⌊2εn⌋`, which preserves the invariant. **Query** for rank `r = ⌈φn⌉` returns the first `v` whose running `r_min` exceeds `r − εn`; the invariant then guarantees `r_max ≤ r + εn`. GK is deterministic by construction (`seed` is accepted for parity). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/gk_quantile_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 91A: `pradyos/core/gk_quantile.py` — `GKError(detail)`; `GKSummary(epsilon=0.01, seed=0)` with `insert(value)` / `insert_many(values)` (numbers only), `query(phi)` → φ-quantile (None if empty; `GKError` on `φ∉[0,1]`), `count()`, `compress()`, `reset(epsilon=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `epsilon` / `seed` / `summary_size` properties, and `stats()` (epsilon / n / summary_size / capacity = `(1/2ε)·log2(2εn)`). Invalid `epsilon` (∉(0,1)) / `seed` / value / `phi` raise `GKError`.
- ✅ 91B: `pradyos/web/gk_quantile_web.py` — `register_gk_quantile_routes(app, gk=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app summary, ε=0.01) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/quantile/insert` (body `{value}` or `{values: [...]}`; 422 on neither / non-list / non-number), `GET /api/v1/quantile/query` (`?phi=`, `Query(ge=0.0, le=1.0)` → 422 on φ∉[0,1]; **422 on empty summary**), `GET /api/v1/quantile/count`, `GET /api/v1/quantile/stats`, `POST /api/v1/quantile/reset` (body `{epsilon?, seed?}`; 422 on bad epsilon).
- ✅ 91C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase91.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `gk_quantile` param, and a single `register_gk_quantile_routes(app, gk_quantile)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 91D: `tests/test_gk_quantile.py` (44) + `tests/test_gk_quantile_web.py` (22) — insert / count / query; median accuracy on 10k uniform (`|est−0.5| ≤ ε + 2/n`); exact min/max; **rank-error guarantee** (every p10–p99 within `εn`, incl. an adversarial sorted stream); monotonicity across 101 quantiles; order-independence of *estimates* (ascending vs reversed); summary-size sub-linear / below `O((1/ε)log(εn))`; ε effect on size; determinism (seed is a no-op — GK has no RNG); epsilon / seed / value / phi validation + `GKError`; stats / capacity / reset / reconfigure; duplicate & negative values; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. empty-summary → 422 + a prior-phase regression check.
- ✅ 91E: `scripts/prove.py` — 199 test modules registered (Phase 91 appends `test_gk_quantile.py` + `test_gk_quantile_web.py`).

**Phase 92 — Complete.** All 201 test modules green. Sovereign KLL Sketch (Karnin–Lang–Liberty, 2016) — a randomized, space-optimal, natively **mergeable** streaming-quantile sketch. It maintains a hierarchy of *compactors* (one list per level `h`); an item stored at level `h` carries weight `2**h`. New items enter level 0; when a compactor reaches capacity `k` it **compacts** — sort, randomly keep the even- or odd-indexed half (a fair coin discards one of each adjacent pair), and promote the survivors up a level. Each compaction conserves total weight, so `Σ 2**h == n` always holds; compaction bounds total stored size to `O(k·log(n/k))` while levels grow as `O(log(n/k))`, giving `O(n/k)` rank error with high probability. **Query** flattens every stored item with its weight, sorts, and returns the weighted-rank `⌈φn⌉` value. **Merge** — the defining advantage over Phase 91's GK — aligns two sketches level-by-level, concatenates the compactors, and re-compacts, combining distributed sketches with the same guarantee. Randomness is per-*compaction* (a `random.Random(seed)` advancing each compaction), so a fixed insert sequence is deterministic. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/kll_sketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 92A: `pradyos/core/kll_sketch.py` — `KLLError(detail)`; `KLLSketch(k=200, seed=0)` with `update(value)` / `update_many(values)`, `query(phi)` → φ-quantile (None if empty; `KLLError` on φ∉[0,1]), `rank(value)` (weighted), `merge(other)` (level-aligned re-compaction), `count()`, `reset(k=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `k` / `seed` / `num_levels` properties, and `stats()` (k / n / num_levels / num_compactors / sketch_size_ratio). Invalid `k` (<2) / `seed` / value / `phi` raise `KLLError`. (Uniform per-level capacity `k`: a starved top compactor would let a few heavy items skew the estimate, so every weight keeps a full-resolution buffer — measured ratio ≈ 0.03 at n=10k.)
- ✅ 92B: `pradyos/web/kll_sketch_web.py` — `register_kll_sketch_routes(app, kll=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch, k=200) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/kll/insert` (body `{value}` or `{values: [...]}`; 422 on neither / non-list / non-number), `GET /api/v1/kll/query` (`?phi=`, `Query(ge=0.0, le=1.0)`; **422 on empty sketch**), `POST /api/v1/kll/merge` (body `{values: [...]}` → builds a temp sketch and merges it in), `GET /api/v1/kll/stats`, `POST /api/v1/kll/reset` (body `{k?, seed?}`; 422 on bad k).
- ✅ 92C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase92.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `kll` param, and a single `register_kll_sketch_routes(app, kll)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 92D: `tests/test_kll_sketch.py` (45) + `tests/test_kll_sketch_web.py` (24) — update / count / query; rank-error guarantee — every p0–p100 (incl. extremes) within `3n/k` on uniform and adversarial sorted streams; monotonicity; weighted `rank()` bounds; **merge** (median accuracy, count combination, preserved rank error, empty-into-populated, non-sketch → `KLLError`); space ratio < 0.1 + level growth + the `Σ weights == n` invariant; determinism (same seed → identical levels); k (<2) / seed / value / phi validation + `KLLError`; stats / reset / reconfigure; duplicate & negative values; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. the merge endpoint + empty → 422 + a prior-phase regression check.
- ✅ 92E: `scripts/prove.py` — 201 test modules registered (Phase 92 appends `test_kll_sketch.py` + `test_kll_sketch_web.py`).
- ✅ 92F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 93 planned.

**Phase 93 — Complete.** All 203 test modules green. Sovereign Theta Sketch (K-Minimum-Values) — distinct-count (cardinality) estimation that, unlike Phase 74's HyperLogLog, supports a **lossless set union** of two sketches. Each element is hashed uniformly into `[0, 1)`; the sketch retains the `k` smallest *distinct* hashes. Once `k` distinct hashes are retained, `θ` is the largest of them (the `k`-th smallest), so `estimate = (k − 1) / θ`; below the threshold the retained count is the exact distinct count. Duplicates hash to an already-retained value and are ignored — repeats never inflate the count. Relative error is `≈ 1/√(k−1)` (≈ 1.6 % at `k = 4096`). **Union** keeps the `k` smallest hashes of the two retained sets (itself a valid KMV sketch of `A ∪ B`); **intersection** follows by inclusion–exclusion `|A ∩ B| ≈ est(A) + est(B) − est(A ∪ B)`. The BLAKE2b hash is seeded for determinism. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/theta_sketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 93A: `pradyos/core/theta_sketch.py` — `ThetaError(detail)`; `ThetaSketch(k=4096, seed=0)` with `update(element)` / `update_many(elements)`, `estimate()` (0 when empty; exact int below `k`), `merge(other)` (mutating union), `union_estimate(other)` / `intersection_estimate(other)` (non-destructive), `reset(k=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `k` / `seed` / `retained_count` / `is_exact` properties, and `stats()` (k / n / theta / retained_count / is_exact / estimate). A max-heap of retained hashes gives O(log k) eviction; a set gives O(1) dedup. Invalid `k` (<2) / `seed` raise `ThetaError`.
- ✅ 93B: `pradyos/web/theta_sketch_web.py` — `register_theta_sketch_routes(app, theta=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch, k=4096) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/theta/insert` (body `{element}` or `{elements: [...]}`; 422 on neither / non-list), `GET /api/v1/theta/estimate` (**0 when empty — never 422**), `POST /api/v1/theta/merge` (`?op=union|intersection`, default union — union mutates & returns `|A∪B|`, intersection is non-destructive & returns `|A∩B|`; 422 on bad op / missing values), `GET /api/v1/theta/stats`, `POST /api/v1/theta/reset` (body `{k?, seed?}`; 422 on bad k).
- ✅ 93C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase93.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `theta` param, and a single `register_theta_sketch_routes(app, theta)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 93D: `tests/test_theta_sketch.py` (45) + `tests/test_theta_sketch_web.py` (24) — 10k-distinct estimate within 5 %; duplicates → exactly 1; exact regime below `k` (estimate == count, `is_exact`); larger-`k` tighter error; **union** (no-overlap → ~2×, full-overlap → ~1×, non-destructive `union_estimate`, count combination, empty/populated edges); **intersection** by inclusion–exclusion (2500-overlap within 10 %, disjoint ≈ 0, full overlap); θ = 1.0 below `k` / <1 when full; retained-count caps at `k`; determinism (same seed → identical retained set) ; k (<2) / seed validation + `ThetaError`; stats / reset / reconfigure; integer elements; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. `op=union|intersection` (incl. non-destructive intersection) + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 94 — Complete.** All 205 test modules green. Sovereign Count Sketch (Charikar–Chen–Farach-Colton, 2002) — sub-linear **frequency** estimation that, unlike Phase 76's Count-Min Sketch, gives an **unbiased** estimate. A `depth × width` integer table is paired with a *bucket* hash `h_i` and a *sign* hash `s_i ∈ {−1, +1}` per row; each `(element, count)` update adds `s_i(element)·count` to `table[i][h_i(element)]`, and a point query returns the **median** of the `depth` signed readings `table[i][h_i(x)]·s_i(x)`. The sign flip makes collision noise cancel in expectation — the estimator is unbiased (vs Count-Min's always-positive `min`, which only over-counts). The trade-off is symmetric noise: a never-inserted element can read a small **negative** estimate when it collides with negatively-signed updates (expected and correct). The median over rows tolerates a few heavily-collided rows; updates accept **negative counts** (deletion). A side dict of every element seen powers `heavy_hitters(threshold)` (the sketch itself is not enumerable). Pure stdlib; the hash families are injectable for tests; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/count_sketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 94A: `pradyos/core/count_sketch.py` — `CountSketchError(detail)`; `CountSketch(depth=5, width=2048, seed=0, bucket_fn=None, sign_fn=None)` with `update(element, count=1)` (count may be negative → deletion), `estimate(element)` (signed median; 0 for unseen in an empty table), `heavy_hitters(threshold)` → elements above `threshold·total_count`, highest first, `reset(depth=None, width=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `depth` / `width` / `seed` / `total_count` / `unique_elements` properties, and `stats()` (depth / width / total_count / unique_elements / table_cells). Two seeded BLAKE2b hash families (bucket + sign); invalid config / non-int count raise `CountSketchError`.
- ✅ 94B: `pradyos/web/count_sketch_web.py` — `register_count_sketch_routes(app, count_sketch=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch, depth 5 × width 2048) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/countsketch/update` (`?count=N`, default 1, may be negative; body `{element}` or `{elements: [...]}`; elements normalised to str), `GET /api/v1/countsketch/estimate` (`?element=`, required → 422 absent; **0 for unseen, never 422**), `GET /api/v1/countsketch/heavy_hitters` (`?threshold=`, `Query(ge=0.0, le=1.0)`), `GET /api/v1/countsketch/stats`, `POST /api/v1/countsketch/reset` (body `{depth?, width?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ✅ 94C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase94.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `count_sketch` param, and a single `register_count_sketch_routes(app, count_sketch)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 94D: `tests/test_count_sketch.py` (41) + `tests/test_count_sketch_web.py` (25) — single-element **unbiasedness** (10k → exactly 10k, no inflation amid 5k singletons); **heavy hitters** on a Zipf stream (top-3 identified & ranked, none above 0.99, sorted desc, threshold validation); **deletion** via negative count (1000−300 → 700, delete-to-zero); **collision tolerance** (2048 elements forced into one row-0 bucket via injected hash → median still recovers 1); **negative estimate** for an unseen colliding element (documented trade-off); determinism (same seed → identical table); depth/width/seed/count validation + `CountSketchError`; stats / table_cells / reset / reconfigure; integer elements; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. `?count=` deletion over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 95 — Complete.** All 207 test modules green. Sovereign Lossy Counting (Manku–Motwani, 2002) — **deterministic** approximate frequency / heavy-hitter detection with a clean ε-error guarantee and *no hashing*. The stream is divided into buckets of width `w = ⌈1/ε⌉`, numbered `1, 2, …`; a dictionary holds `{element: (freq, Δ)}` where `Δ` bounds the count's under-estimate. On each arrival the element's `freq` is incremented, or it is inserted as `(count, b_current − 1)`; at every bucket boundary the table is swept and every entry with `freq + Δ ≤ b_current` is deleted. This guarantees **no false negatives** (every element with true frequency ≥ `support·n` is returned by `heavy_hitters(support)`), **no false positives above threshold** (every returned element has true frequency ≥ `(support − ε)·n`), and a **space bound** of `(1/ε)·log(εn)` entries. The algorithm is fully deterministic (no RNG — `seed` is accepted for parity but unused), and **append-only**: a negative `count` raises `LossyCountError` (deletion is unsupported by design). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/lossy_count_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 95A: `pradyos/core/lossy_count.py` — `LossyCountError(detail)`; `LossyCount(epsilon=0.001, seed=None)` with `update(element, count=1)` (negative count → `LossyCountError("…does not support deletion")`; count=0 is a no-op), `estimate(element)` → tracked frequency (0 if absent), `heavy_hitters(support)` → elements with freq ≥ `(support − ε)·n`, highest first, `reset(epsilon=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `epsilon` / `bucket_width` / `n` / `entries` properties, and `stats()` (epsilon / n / bucket_width / entries / current_bucket). The bucket-boundary sweep loop handles batch counts crossing multiple boundaries. Invalid `epsilon` (∉(0,1)) / non-int count raise `LossyCountError`.
- ✅ 95B: `pradyos/web/lossy_count_web.py` — `register_lossy_count_routes(app, lossy=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app counter, ε=0.001) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/lossycount/update` (`?count=N`; body `{element}` or `{elements: [...]}`; **negative count → 422 "does not support deletion"**; elements normalised to str), `GET /api/v1/lossycount/estimate` (`?element=`, required → 422 absent; 0 if not retained), `GET /api/v1/lossycount/heavy_hitters` (`?support=`, `Query(gt=0, le=1.0)`), `GET /api/v1/lossycount/stats`, `POST /api/v1/lossycount/reset` (body `{epsilon?}`; 422 on bad epsilon).
- ✅ 95C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase95.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `lossy` param, and a single `register_lossy_count_routes(app, lossy)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 95D: `tests/test_lossy_count.py` (43) + `tests/test_lossy_count_web.py` (24) — uniform stream (1% elements below 5% → empty; all 100 returned at 0.5%; exact estimate); **Zipf no-false-negatives** + correct ranking + **no-false-positives-above-threshold** (every returned element ≥ `(support−ε)·n`); estimate never over-counts & under-count ≤ `ε·n`; single-element exact; **bucket-sweep invariant** (no entry with `freq+Δ ≤ b_current`); sub-linear space; rare elements swept; **no-deletion guard** (negative → `LossyCountError`, count=0 no-op, non-int rejected); determinism (seed ignored → identical state); epsilon / support validation + `LossyCountError`; stats / reset / reconfigure; integer elements; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. negative-count → 422 over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.
- ✅ 95E: `scripts/prove.py` — 207 test modules registered (Phase 95 appends `test_lossy_count.py` + `test_lossy_count_web.py`).

**Phase 96 — Complete.** All 209 test modules green. Sovereign DDSketch (Masson–Lee, 2019) — a **relative-error** quantile sketch (a different guarantee from the *rank*-error sketches of Phases 91/92). Each positive value `v` is mapped to a logarithmic bucket `i = ⌈log_γ(v)⌉` with `γ = (1+α)/(1−α)`, and a dict `{bucket → count}` tallies them; a quantile query walks the buckets in value order to the `q`-th item and returns that bucket's representative value `r_i = 2·γ**i/(γ+1)` (the geometric midpoint, whose worst-case relative error is exactly `(γ−1)/(γ+1) = α`). So for any quantile `q` with true value `v`, the estimate satisfies `|v̂ − v|/v ≤ α` regardless of distribution — ideal for long-tailed latencies where p99 accuracy matters proportionally. **Merge** adds per-bucket counts of two same-`α` sketches — *exact*, not approximate (the key differentiator over t-Digest), so distributed sketches compose losslessly. Deterministic (`seed` accepted but unused); non-positive values are rejected. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/ddsketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 96A: `pradyos/core/ddsketch.py` — `DDSketchError(detail)`; `DDSketch(alpha=0.01, seed=None)` with `update(value, count=1)` (value > 0 or `DDSketchError("DDSketch requires positive values")`; count ≥ 1), `quantile(q)` → relative-error estimate (None if empty; `DDSketchError` on q∉[0,1]), `merge(other)` (exact bucket-count union; same `α` or `DDSketchError`), `reset(alpha=None, seed=None)`, `count()`, `__len__`, `alpha` / `gamma` / `num_buckets` properties, and `stats()` (alpha / gamma / n / num_buckets / min / max). Representative value uses the standard `2·γ**i/(γ+1)` (which bounds relative error by `α`) — not a naive `(1+α)**i`, which mixes bases and would not bound the error. Invalid `alpha` (∉(0,1)) raises `DDSketchError`.
- ✅ 96B: `pradyos/web/ddsketch_web.py` — `register_ddsketch_routes(app, ddsketch=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch, α=0.01) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/ddsketch/update` (`?value=` `Query(gt=0)` → **422 on non-positive**, `?count=` `Query(ge=1)`, or body `{values: [...]}`), `GET /api/v1/ddsketch/quantile` (`?q=`, `Query(ge=0, le=1)`; **422 on empty sketch**), `POST /api/v1/ddsketch/merge` (body `{values: [...]}` → builds a same-`α` sketch and merges it in — the single-shared-sketch server's composability demonstration), `GET /api/v1/ddsketch/stats`, `POST /api/v1/ddsketch/reset` (body `{alpha?}`; 422 on bad alpha).
- ✅ 96C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase96.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `ddsketch` param, and a single `register_ddsketch_routes(app, ddsketch)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 96D: `tests/test_ddsketch.py` (45) + `tests/test_ddsketch_web.py` (24) — uniform & exponential & wide-range (1..1e6) streams with **every quantile level within `α` relative error**; monotonicity; extremes within `α`; **exact merge** (merged sketch identical to a single sketch of all values) + preserved relative error + min/max update + alpha-mismatch/non-sketch → `DDSketchError`; non-positive value guard (`update(0)`/`update(-1)` raise) + invalid count; determinism (seed ignored); alpha / q validation + `gamma` formula; stats / sub-linear bucket count / reset / reconfigure; floats below 1; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. the merge endpoint + empty → 422 + a prior-phase regression check.
- ✅ 96E: `scripts/prove.py` — 209 test modules registered (Phase 96 appends `test_ddsketch.py` + `test_ddsketch_web.py`).

**Phase 97 — Complete.** All 211 test modules green. Sovereign Exponential Histogram (Datar–Gionis–Indyk–Motwani, 2002) — the first **sliding-window** primitive: how many 1-bits occurred in the last `window` ticks of a binary stream, in `O((1/ε)·log²(window))` space (it never stores the raw stream). The window is summarised by buckets `(timestamp, size=2ᵏ)` ordered oldest→newest; each update appends a size-1 bucket at the current tick, then — while more than `k = ⌈1/ε⌉` buckets share a size — merges the two **oldest** of that size into one of double the size (taking the newer timestamp); buckets older than `window` ticks expire. `count()` returns `Σ size − ½·(oldest bucket size)` (the DGIM end-correction, since the oldest bucket may straddle the boundary), estimating the windowed count with **relative error ≤ ε/2** (empirically validated). Deterministic (`seed` accepted but unused); a binary-stream model (`value` = number of 1-bits at a tick; no fractional/weighted updates). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/exponential_histogram_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 97A: `pradyos/core/exponential_histogram.py` — `ExponentialHistogramError(detail)`; `ExponentialHistogram(window, epsilon=0.5, seed=None)` with `update(value=1, timestamp=None)` (value ≥ 1 1-bits; timestamp defaults to the next internal tick, must be non-decreasing else `ExponentialHistogramError`), `count()` → DGIM windowed estimate, `oldest()` → oldest surviving bucket timestamp (None if empty), `reset(window=None, epsilon=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `window` / `epsilon` / `k` / `now` / `num_buckets` properties, and `stats()` (window / epsilon / k / num_buckets / count / oldest / now). Invalid `window` (≤0) / `epsilon` (∉(0,1]) raise `ExponentialHistogramError`.
- ✅ 97B: `pradyos/web/exponential_histogram_web.py` — `register_exponential_histogram_routes(app, histogram=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app histogram, window=1000) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/window/update` (`?value=` `Query(ge=1)`, `?timestamp=` `Query(ge=0)`; **422 on non-monotone timestamp**), `GET /api/v1/window/count`, `GET /api/v1/window/oldest`, `GET /api/v1/window/stats`, `POST /api/v1/window/reset` (`?window=` `Query(gt=0)`, `?epsilon=` `Query(gt=0, le=1)`; 422 on bad params).
- ✅ 97C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase97.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `exp_histogram` param, and a single `register_exponential_histogram_routes(app, exp_histogram)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 97D: `tests/test_exponential_histogram.py` (42) + `tests/test_exponential_histogram_web.py` (20) — dense count within `ε/2` (incl. the directive's window=500/ε=0.5 scenario, tighter ε, and sub-window n); **sliding expiry** (200 then advance 600 then 100 → ~100); old-buckets-expire + expiry invariant + oldest-advances; **merge invariant** (≤ `k+1` buckets per size after every update) + power-of-two sizes + poly-log space; explicit timestamps + multi-bit `value`; determinism (seed ignored); window/epsilon/value/non-monotone-timestamp validation + `ExponentialHistogramError`; stats / reset / reconfigure; the single-bit DGIM end-correction (`count`=0.5); 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. sliding expiry over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.
- ✅ 97E: `scripts/prove.py` — 211 test modules registered (Phase 97 appends `test_exponential_histogram.py` + `test_exponential_histogram_web.py`).

**Phase 98 — Complete.** All 213 test modules green. Sovereign Weighted Reservoir Sampling (Efraimidis–Spirakis "A-Res", 2006) — a random sample of `k` items from a stream of `(item, weight)` pairs in one pass and `O(k)` space, where an item is retained with probability **proportional to its weight** (unlike Phase 85's *uniform* Algorithm R). Each arrival gets a priority key `u**(1/weight)` (`u ∼ Uniform(0,1)`); a **min-heap** keeps the `k` items with the largest keys (push while under capacity, else replace the smallest if beaten). Heavier weights drive `1/weight` toward 0 and thus the key toward 1, so heavy items win more — verified empirically at a ~96:1 selection ratio for weight 100 vs 1. This is the first **randomized** primitive in a while: a seeded `random.Random` makes it reproducible/injectable. `reset()` clears the reservoir but deliberately does *not* re-seed the RNG (the generator state continues — correct for a long-lived sampler). A counter tiebreaker `(key, counter, item)` means the heap never compares items, so any item type is safe. Weights must be positive; `k ≥ 1`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/weighted_reservoir_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 98A: `pradyos/core/weighted_reservoir.py` — `WeightedReservoirError(detail)`; `WeightedReservoir(k, seed=0)` with `update(item, weight=1.0)` (weight > 0 or `WeightedReservoirError("weight must be positive")`), `sample()` → reservoir contents (`[]` if empty, order not guaranteed), `reset()` (clears; RNG continues), `__len__`, `k` / `seed` / `n` / `size` properties, and `stats()` (k / n / size / seed). `k < 1` raises `WeightedReservoirError("k must be at least 1")`. No `merge` — A-Res reservoirs are not composable.
- ✅ 98B: `pradyos/web/weighted_reservoir_web.py` — `register_weighted_reservoir_routes(app, reservoir=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sampler, k=100) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/sample/update` (`?item=` required str, `?weight=` `Query(gt=0)` → **422 on non-positive**), `GET /api/v1/sample/sample` (`{items, n, k}`), `GET /api/v1/sample/stats`, `POST /api/v1/sample/reset`.
- ✅ 98C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase98.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `weighted_reservoir` param, and a single `register_weighted_reservoir_routes(app, weighted_reservoir)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 98D: `tests/test_weighted_reservoir.py` (35) + `tests/test_weighted_reservoir_web.py` (18) — capacity fills to `k` (10k items → 50) / under-capacity keeps all / exactly-k; **weight-proportional bias** (weight 100 selected >10× weight 1; top-10 by frequency all from the top-20 by weight) + uniform-weights-unbiased; determinism (same seed → identical reservoir) + different-seed-differs; **reset does not re-seed the RNG** (replay diverges from a fresh same-seed reservoir); weight guard (0 / negative / non-number raise) + `k`/`seed` validation + `WeightedReservoirError`; arbitrary non-comparable item types (counter tiebreaker); stats / reset / refill; 10-thread concurrency; all 4 endpoints incl. injected capacity + a high-weight-retained check + a prior-phase regression check.
- ✅ 98E: `scripts/prove.py` — 213 test modules registered (Phase 98 appends `test_weighted_reservoir.py` + `test_weighted_reservoir_web.py`).
- ✅ 98F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 99 planned.

**Phase 99 — Complete.** All 215 test modules green. Sovereign Misra-Gries (Misra–Gries, 1982) — the original **deterministic counter-based heavy-hitter** algorithm. At most `k` monitored `(item → count)` counters are kept: on a hit increment; on a new item with a free slot start a counter; otherwise **decrement every counter** by the item's count and drop those that reach zero (the arriving item is absorbed by that decrement, not stored). This is the distinctive Misra-Gries step — compared with Space-Saving's *evict-minimum* (P87) and Lossy Counting's *window-sweep* (P95). Guarantees: any element with true frequency `> n/(k+1)` is retained; every reported count under-estimates the true frequency by at most `n/(k+1)`; space is exactly `k` counters. So `heavy_hitters(support)` (counts `≥ (support − 1/(k+1))·n`) has no false negatives among elements with true frequency `≥ support·n` **provided `support > 1/(k+1)`** (a larger `k` covers smaller support). Deterministic (no RNG — `seed` accepted but unused); append-only (non-positive `count` raises `MisraGriesError`). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/misra_gries_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 99A: `pradyos/core/misra_gries.py` — `MisraGriesError(detail)`; `MisraGries(k, seed=None)` with `update(element, count=1)` (count ≥ 1; non-positive → `MisraGriesError("Misra-Gries does not support deletion")`), `estimate(element)` → stored under-count (0 if absent), `heavy_hitters(support)` → elements with count `≥ (support − 1/(k+1))·n`, highest first, `reset(k=None)`, `__len__`, `k` / `n` / `counters` properties, and `stats()` (k / n / counters / `threshold = n/(k+1)`). `k < 1` raises `MisraGriesError("k must be at least 1")`.
- ✅ 99B: `pradyos/web/misra_gries_web.py` — `register_misra_gries_routes(app, misra=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app counter, k=100) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/misragries/update` (`?count=` `Query(ge=1)` → **422 on non-positive (the no-deletion guard)**; body `{element}` or `{elements: [...]}`), `GET /api/v1/misragries/estimate` (`?element=`, required → 422 absent), `GET /api/v1/misragries/heavy_hitters` (`?support=`, `Query(gt=0, le=1)`), `GET /api/v1/misragries/stats`, `POST /api/v1/misragries/reset` (body `{k?}`; 422 on bad k).
- ✅ 99C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase99.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `misra_gries` param, and a single `register_misra_gries_routes(app, misra_gries)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.

**Phase 100 — Complete. 🎯 Centennial.** All 217 test modules green. Sovereign XOR Filter (Graf–Lemire, 2020) — a **static, space-optimal** approximate-membership filter that beats Bloom (P72) and Cuckoo (P86) on lookup speed (exactly **three memory probes, no search**) and is built **once** from a complete key set (then immutable — the design difference from the incremental Bloom and Cuckoo). Each key maps to three buckets `h0, h1, h2` (one per segment); a **peeling** construction repeatedly removes a key that owns a bucket no other unassigned key touches, then assigns fingerprints in reverse peel order so `F[b] = fingerprint(k) ⊕ F[other1] ⊕ F[other2]` — making `fingerprint(k) == F[h0] ⊕ F[h1] ⊕ F[h2]` hold for every built key (zero false negatives). A non-member matches with probability `≈ 2**-bits_per_entry` (≈ 0.4 % at 8 bits, 0 observed at 16 bits over 10 000 queries). Fingerprints are the low `bits_per_entry` bits of a seeded BLAKE2b digest. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/xor_filter_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 100A: `pradyos/core/xor_filter.py` — `XorFilterError(detail)`; `XorFilter(bits_per_entry=8, seed=0)` with `build(keys)` (static; dedups; replaces any prior filter; `XorFilterError("peeling failed — retry with different seed")` on a rare stall), `contains(key)` (`XorFilterError("filter not built — call build() first")` before build), `reset(bits_per_entry=None, seed=None)`, `__contains__`, `__len__`, `bits_per_entry` / `seed` / `built` / `array_size` properties, and `stats()` (bits_per_entry / built / n / array_size / segment_size / `false_positive_rate = 2**-bits`). Invalid `bits_per_entry` (∉[1,64]) / `seed` raise `XorFilterError`.
- ✅ 100B: `pradyos/web/xor_filter_web.py` — `register_xor_filter_routes(app, xor=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app filter, 8-bit, unbuilt) mounts 4 (all-static) routes — **no insert (the filter is static)**: `POST /api/v1/xorfilter/build` (body `{keys: [...]}`; 422 on missing / non-list / peeling failure), `GET /api/v1/xorfilter/contains` (`?key=`; **422 before build**), `GET /api/v1/xorfilter/stats`, `POST /api/v1/xorfilter/reset` (body `{bits_per_entry?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ✅ 100C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase100.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `xor_filter` param, and a single `register_xor_filter_routes(app, xor_filter)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 100D: `tests/test_xor_filter.py` (39) + `tests/test_xor_filter_web.py` (20) — membership (10 000 keys all contained, zero false negatives); 8-bit FPR `< 1/128` & 16-bit FPR `0`/10 000 & wider-fingerprint-fewer-FPs; **static constraint** (contains before build / after reset raises); **rebuild replaces** (set A → set B; A survives only at FP level); `build` dedups; determinism (same seed → identical array) + different-seed-differs; **peeling robustness** (0 failures across 20 varied key sets at one seed); bits / seed validation + `XorFilterError`; stats / FPR formula / reset / reconfigure; integer & mixed key types; 10-thread concurrent membership; all 4 endpoints incl. build → contains over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.
- ✅ 100E: `scripts/prove.py` — 217 test modules registered (Phase 100 appends `test_xor_filter.py` + `test_xor_filter_web.py`).

**Phase 101 — Complete.** All 219 test modules green. Sovereign Ribbon Filter (Dillinger–Walzer, 2021) — the **retrieval-based** static membership filter that succeeds the XOR filter (P100) with better space efficiency: it frames membership as a **sparse linear system over GF(2)** and solves it down a narrow diagonal *ribbon* band rather than by peeling. Each key maps to a start column `s(k) ∈ [0, m-w]`, a `w`-bit coefficient row `c(k)` anchored at `s` (bit 0 forced to 1), and a `bits_per_entry`-bit fingerprint `f(k)`; its equation is `⊕_{j: c(k)[j]=1} Z[s(k)+j] = f(k)` over a slot table `Z`. Rows are reduced into an incremental row-echelon form keyed by pivot column (each insert shifts to its leftmost set bit and, if that pivot is occupied, XORs against the resident row — the band never widens past `w`, so each insert is `O(w)`), then a back-substitution from the high column down fills `Z`. A query recomputes `s, c` and XORs the selected slots, so `⊕ Z[s+j] == f(k)` holds for every built key (**zero false negatives**); a non-member matches only by fingerprint collision (`≈ 2**-bits`, ≈ 0.4 % at 8 bits, 0 observed at 16 bits over 10 000 queries). With ribbon width `w = 64` and target load `0.85`, the table is `m = ⌈n / 0.85⌉ + w` slots — an overhead of **≈ 1.18× at scale, below the XOR filter's 1.23× theoretical bound and far below its 3.69× peeling construction**; wider `w` pushes the load toward the `n · bits` limit. If a row reduces to zero coefficients with a non-zero residual the system is singular — `RibbonFilterError` asks for a different seed (astronomically rare at load 0.85). Fingerprint / start / coefficient are slices of a seeded BLAKE2b digest. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock` (the heavy solve runs lock-free on a snapshot, published with one locked assignment). Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/ribbon_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 101A: `pradyos/core/ribbon.py` — `RibbonFilterError(detail)`; `RibbonFilter(bits_per_entry=8, seed=0)` with `build(keys)` (static; dedups; replaces any prior filter; `RibbonFilterError("construction failed — linearly dependent rows (retry with different seed)")` on a singular system; empty build is valid and contains nothing), `contains(key)` (`RibbonFilterError("filter not built — call build() first")` before build), `reset(bits_per_entry=None, seed=None)`, `__contains__`, `__len__`, `bits_per_entry` / `seed` / `built` / `slots` / `ribbon_width` properties, and `stats()` (bits_per_entry / built / n / slots / ribbon_width / load_factor / `false_positive_rate = 2**-bits`). Invalid `bits_per_entry` (∉[1,64]) / `seed` raise `RibbonFilterError`.
- ✅ 101B: `pradyos/web/ribbon_web.py` — `register_ribbon_routes(app, ribbon=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app filter, 8-bit, unbuilt) mounts 4 (all-static) routes — **no insert (the filter is static)**: `POST /api/v1/ribbon/build` (body `{keys: [...]}`; 422 on missing / non-list / singular-system), `GET /api/v1/ribbon/contains` (`?key=`; **422 before build**), `GET /api/v1/ribbon/stats`, `POST /api/v1/ribbon/reset` (body `{bits_per_entry?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ✅ 101C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase101.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `ribbon_filter` param, and a single `register_ribbon_routes(app, ribbon_filter)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 101D: `tests/test_ribbon.py` (40) + `tests/test_ribbon_web.py` (21) — membership (5 000 keys all contained, zero false negatives); 8-bit FPR `< 1/128` & 16-bit FPR `0`/5 000 & fewer-FPs-at-more-bits; **static constraint** (contains before build / after reset raises); **rebuild replaces**; `build` dedups; **GF(2) solve robustness** (0 construction failures across 20 varied key sets, incl. n = 1…7 000); determinism (same seed → identical slot table) + different-seed-differs; **sizing** (`m = ⌈n/0.85⌉+64`; overhead `< 1.23×` at n = 10 000); bits / seed validation + `RibbonFilterError.detail`; stats / FPR formula / load_factor / reset / reconfigure; integer & mixed key types; empty build; 10-thread concurrent membership; all 4 endpoints incl. build → contains over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.
- ✅ 101E: `scripts/prove.py` — 219 test modules registered (Phase 101 appends `test_ribbon.py` + `test_ribbon_web.py`).
- ✅ 101F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 102 planned.

**Phase 102 — Complete.** All 221 test modules green. Sovereign HeavyKeeper (Gong et al., 2018) — a probabilistic **heavy-hitter / top-K frequency** sketch (pivot: the originally-eyed Count-Min Sketch was already shipped at P76 — `class CountMinSketch` — so Phase 102 stays in the frequency family but ships a genuinely-new algorithm). It keeps a `depth × width` grid of `(fingerprint, count)` cells (`count == 0` marks empty); for each occurrence of an item `x` (fingerprint `f = fp(x)`), every row hashes `x` to a cell and applies **exponential-decay-on-collision**: an empty cell is claimed `(f, 1)`, a matching fingerprint does `count += 1`, and a *mismatching* cell decays the resident only with probability `decay ** -count` — evicting and re-claiming it when the count hits 0. Because a genuine heavy hitter's count is large, `decay ** -count` is minuscule, so it is almost never decayed while cold items evaporate fast. The frequency estimate is the **max** matching counter across rows (not the *min*, as in Count-Min P76 — decay makes over-counting the failure mode to guard), and a bounded **indexed min-heap of size k** (`O(log k)` updates) tracks the live top-K, replacing its minimum only when exceeded. This decay rule is the distinctive mechanism — versus Count-Min's *min counters* (P76), Count Sketch's *signed estimate* (P94), Space-Saving's *evict-minimum* (P87), Misra-Gries' *decrement-all* (P99) and Lossy Counting's *window-sweep* (P95). Hashing is seeded BLAKE2b; the decay draws from a seeded `random.Random` so `seed` + stream is fully deterministic. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/heavykeeper_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 102A: `pradyos/core/heavykeeper.py` — `HeavyKeeperError(detail)`; `HeavyKeeper(k=10, width=1024, depth=4, decay=1.08, seed=0)` with `add(item, count=1)` (returns the updated estimate; reconciles the top-K heap), `query(item)` (max matching counter, 0 if absent), `top_k(n=None)` (`(item, estimate)` sorted by estimate desc; defaults to `k`), `reset(k=None, width=None, depth=None, decay=None, seed=None)` (clears buckets + heap; optional reconfigure), `__len__` (tracked count), `k`/`width`/`depth`/`decay`/`seed` properties, and `stats()` (k / width / depth / decay / seed / tracked / total). Invalid `k`/`width`/`depth` (∉ ℤ⁺), `decay` (≤ 1) or `seed` / non-positive `count` raise `HeavyKeeperError`.
- ✅ 102B: `pradyos/web/heavykeeper_web.py` — `register_heavykeeper_routes(app, heavykeeper=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/heavykeeper/add` (body `{item, count?}`; 422 on missing item / bad count), `GET /api/v1/heavykeeper/topk` (`?n=` with `Query(ge=1)` → auto-422; defaults to `k`), `GET /api/v1/heavykeeper/stats`, `POST /api/v1/heavykeeper/reset` (body `{k?, width?, depth?, decay?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ✅ 102C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase102.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `heavykeeper` param, and a single `register_heavykeeper_routes(app, heavykeeper)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 102D: `tests/test_heavykeeper.py` (41) + `tests/test_heavykeeper_web.py` (20) — **heavy-hitter detection** (1 @ 1000 + 9 @ 100 in a 10 000 stream → all 10 in `top_k(10)`); **frequency accuracy** (top item within 20 % of 1000); **eviction** (freq < 5 noise never in top-K); **decay sensitivity** (decay 1.02 forgets faster → less surviving bucket mass & lower hot-item counts than 1.5); **estimate = max not min**; determinism (same seed + stream → identical top-K, survives reset); top-K bounded by `k` / sorted desc / `n` param / keeps-largest; config + `count` validation + `HeavyKeeperError.detail`; stats / reset / reconfigure; integer & mixed items; 8-thread concurrent adds (heap ≤ k, index map consistent, dominant hitter retained); all 4 endpoints over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.
- ✅ 102E: `scripts/prove.py` — 221 test modules registered (Phase 102 appends `test_heavykeeper.py` + `test_heavykeeper_web.py`).

**Phase 103 — Complete.** All 223 test modules green. Sovereign Spectral Bloom Filter (Cohen & Matias, 2003) — a **frequency-aware** Bloom filter that replaces the standard filter's single presence *bit* (P12) with an array of integer **counters**, estimating an item's multiplicity as the **minimum** counter across its `k` hash positions. That minimum is the natural estimator and the exact counterpoint to HeavyKeeper's *max* (P102): collisions can only push a counter higher, so the smallest of an item's counters is the tightest estimate and over-counting (never under-counting) is the only failure mode — zero false negatives, like any Bloom. Because the cells are counters, it also supports **deletion**: `remove` decrements an item's counters (guarded so a non-member, whose minimum is already 0, is never touched and counters never go negative) — the practical edge over a plain Bloom. Sizing uses the standard Bloom formulae from `capacity` and `error_rate`: `m = ⌈-capacity·ln(error_rate)/ln(2)²⌉` counter slots and `k = round((m/capacity)·ln2)` hashes, so membership FPR (`min > 0`) equals a standard Bloom's. The `k` positions come from one seeded BLAKE2b digest split into two 64-bit halves combined by Kirsch–Mitzenmacher double hashing (`h1 + i·h2 mod m`), deterministic per `seed`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/spectralbloom_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 103A: `pradyos/core/spectral_bloom.py` — `SpectralBloomError(detail)`; `SpectralBloom(capacity=10000, error_rate=0.01, seed=0)` with `add(element, count=1)` (returns the updated multiplicity estimate), `query(element)` (min counter; 0 if absent), `remove(element, count=1)` (removes up to `count` occurrences only if present; returns the number removed; guards ≥ 0), `reset(capacity=None, error_rate=None, seed=None)` (clears; re-derives `m`/`k`), `__contains__` (min > 0), `__len__` (net occurrences), `capacity`/`error_rate`/`seed`/`num_bits`/`num_hashes` properties, and `stats()` (capacity / error_rate / num_bits / num_hashes / num_added / estimated_fill_ratio). Invalid `capacity` (∉ ℤ⁺), `error_rate` (∉ (0,1)) or `seed`, and non-positive `count`, raise `SpectralBloomError`.
- ✅ 103B: `pradyos/web/spectralbloom_web.py` — `register_spectralbloom_routes(app, spectral=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app filter) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/spectralbloom/add` (body `{item, count?}`), `GET /api/v1/spectralbloom/query` (`?item=` → auto-422 if absent), `DELETE /api/v1/spectralbloom/remove` (body `{item, count?}` — deletion), `GET /api/v1/spectralbloom/stats`, `POST /api/v1/spectralbloom/reset` (body `{capacity?, error_rate?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ✅ 103C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase103.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `spectral_bloom` param, and a single `register_spectralbloom_routes(app, spectral_bloom)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 103D: `tests/test_spectral_bloom.py` (43) + `tests/test_spectralbloom_web.py` (21) — **zero false negatives** (1 000 members all query ≥ 1); **FPR ≤ 2 × error_rate** (and near-0 under-loaded); **multiplicity exact at low load** (add ×5 → query 5; batch `add(x, 7)`); **estimate = min not max**; **deletion** (add 3 → remove → 2 → remove to 0/not-member; remove non-member is a no-op that never corrupts shared counters; over-remove clamped); standard Bloom sizing (`m`/`k` formulae; smaller error_rate grows `m`); determinism (same seed → identical positions, survives reset); config + `count` validation + `SpectralBloomError.detail`; stats / num_added / fill_ratio / reset / reconfigure; membership operator; integer & mixed items; 8-thread concurrent adds (no lost increments); all 5 endpoints incl. `DELETE`-with-body over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.
- ✅ 103E: `scripts/prove.py` — 223 test modules registered (Phase 103 appends `test_spectral_bloom.py` + `test_spectralbloom_web.py`).

**Phase 104 — Complete.** All 225 test modules green. Sovereign Augmented Sketch / ASketch (Roy, Khan & Pomerantz, 2016) — a **two-stage frequency** estimator that bolts a small *exact* filter of the current heavy hitters onto a sketch base (pivot: the directive's eyed Cuckoo Filter is already shipped at P86 — `class CuckooFilter`, `/api/v1/cuckoo` — so Phase 104 ships a genuinely-new structure). **Stage 1** is a **Count Sketch** base (Charikar–Chen–Farach-Colton 2002), *not* Count-Min (P76): each of `depth` rows maps an item to a bucket and an independent **sign** `s ∈ {+1,-1}`, `add` does `counter[d][j] += s·delta`, and the estimate is the **median** of `s·counter[d][j]` across rows — a *signed median*, so colliding items contribute `±` and cancel in expectation (an *unbiased* estimate), where Count-Min's min only ever over-counts. **Stage 2** is an exact-count dict of ≤ `k` items: on `add`, a tracked item's count is bumped exactly, otherwise the sketch is updated and the item is **promoted** (evicting the dict minimum when full) once its sketch estimate exceeds the smallest tracked count; `query` returns the exact dict count when tracked, else the sketch median, and `top_k` reads exact counts straight off the dict. Hashing is seeded BLAKE2b (one digest per row → bucket + sign bit). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/augmentedsketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 104A: `pradyos/core/augmented_sketch.py` — `AugmentedSketchError(detail)`; `AugmentedSketch(width=1024, depth=4, k=10, seed=0)` with `add(item, delta=1)` (returns updated estimate; promotes into the dict), `query(item)` (exact if tracked, else signed-median sketch estimate), `sketch_estimate(item)` (the Count Sketch base estimate alone), `top_k(n=None)` (`(item, exact_count)` desc; defaults to `k`), `reset(width=None, depth=None, k=None, seed=None)`, `__len__` (tracked count), `width`/`depth`/`k`/`seed` properties, and `stats()` (width / depth / k / seed / tracked / total). Invalid `width`/`depth`/`k` (∉ ℤ⁺) or `seed`, and non-positive `delta`, raise `AugmentedSketchError`.
- ✅ 104B: `pradyos/web/augmentedsketch_web.py` — `register_augmentedsketch_routes(app, augmented=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/augmentedsketch/add` (body `{item, delta?}`; 422 on missing item / bad delta), `GET /api/v1/augmentedsketch/query` (`?item=` → auto-422 if absent), `GET /api/v1/augmentedsketch/topk` (`?n=` with `Query(ge=1)`; defaults to `k`), `GET /api/v1/augmentedsketch/stats`, `POST /api/v1/augmentedsketch/reset` (body `{width?, depth?, k?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ✅ 104C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase104.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `augmented_sketch` param, and a single `register_augmentedsketch_routes(app, augmented_sketch)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 104D: `tests/test_augmented_sketch.py` (39) + `tests/test_augmentedsketch_web.py` (22) — **heavy-hitter detection** (1 @ 1000 + 4 @ 100 in a 10 000 stream → all in `top_k`, counts within 50 of true since promoted); **sketch quality** (mid-frequency signed-median within ~30 %); **sign cancellation** (Count Sketch base estimate of an item stays ≈ its true count under heavy colliding noise — not inflated as Count-Min's min would be); **promotion** (a riser transitions from sketch estimate to exact dict count; a light item is not promoted past a full dict); top-K bounded by `k` / sorted desc / `n` param / keeps-largest; determinism (same seed + stream → identical top-K and sketch array; survives reset); config + `delta` validation + `AugmentedSketchError.detail`; stats / reset / reconfigure; integer & mixed items; 8-thread concurrent adds (dict ≤ k, dominant hitter retained); all 5 endpoints over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.
- ✅ 104E: `scripts/prove.py` — 225 test modules registered (Phase 104 appends `test_augmented_sketch.py` + `test_augmentedsketch_web.py`).
- ✅ 104F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 105 planned.

**Phase 105 — Complete.** All 227 test modules green. Sovereign Q-Digest (Shrivastava, Buragohain, Agrawal & Suri, 2004) — a **mergeable quantile sketch** for streaming percentile estimation (p50/p95/p99). It lays a *complete binary tree* over the value universe `[0, value_range)` (rounded up to a power-of-two capacity so the tree is complete), each node spanning `[lower, upper)`; only nodes with a positive count are stored (a `dict` keyed by heap-numbered node id), so the empty regions of a sparse universe cost nothing. `add` increments the value's leaf, then **compresses**: with `n` total elements and factor `k` the threshold is `⌊n/k⌋`, and the tree is swept bottom-up merging any node/sibling/parent triple whose summed count falls below it up into the parent — enforcing the digest property and bounding the structure to `O(k·log σ)` nodes (`σ = value_range`). `quantile(q)` walks stored nodes by increasing upper boundary, accumulating counts until the running sum reaches `q·n`, and reports that node's max value; `rank(v)` sums counts of nodes lying entirely at/below `v`; `merge` adds node counts of two same-universe digests and recompresses (ideal for distributed aggregation). Fully deterministic (no randomness; the `seed` is carried for API parity and reported in stats). *(Pivot note: the directive's eyed **t-Digest is already shipped at Phase 79** — `class TDigest`, `/api/v1/tdigest` — and **DDSketch at Phase 96** — `/api/v1/ddsketch`; both quantile sketches collide, so Phase 105 ships a genuinely-new one, distinct from those plus Greenwald-Khanna (P91) and KLL (P92) — a tree/domain-decomposition approach.)* Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/qdigest_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 105A: `pradyos/core/q_digest.py` — `QDigestError(detail)`; `QDigest(compression_factor=100, value_range=65536, seed=0)` with `add(value, count=1)` (range-checked; recompresses), `quantile(q)` (`q` strictly in (0,1); `QDigestError` on empty / bad `q`), `rank(value)`, `merge(other)` (same-universe node-wise add + recompress; returns self; does not mutate `other`), `reset(compression_factor=None, value_range=None, seed=None)`, `__len__` (total count), `compression_factor`/`value_range`/`seed`/`num_nodes`/`total_count` properties, and `stats()` (compression_factor / value_range / total_count / num_nodes / theoretical_max_nodes = `k·log σ`). Invalid config, out-of-range / non-int value, or non-positive count raise `QDigestError`.
- ✅ 105B: `pradyos/web/qdigest_web.py` — `register_qdigest_routes(app, qdigest=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app digest) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/qdigest/add` (body `{value, count?}`; 422 on missing value / out-of-range / bad count), `GET /api/v1/qdigest/quantile` (`?q=` with `Query(gt=0.0, lt=1.0)`; **422 on empty digest**), `POST /api/v1/qdigest/merge` (body `{values: [...]}` → builds a temp digest and merges it in), `GET /api/v1/qdigest/stats`, `POST /api/v1/qdigest/reset` (body `{compression_factor?, value_range?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).

Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 105D: `tests/test_q_digest.py` (64) + `tests/test_qdigest_web.py` (24) — **uniform p50** (10 000 values over [0,1000) → p50 ∈ [475,525]); **tail p99** within 5 % of 990; **merge correctness** (two 5 000-value halves → merged p50 within 5 % of true); **compression bound** (`num_nodes ≤ 4·k·log₂(value_range)`); **strict monotonicity** of `quantile(0.25..0.99)`; **determinism** (same seed + values + order → identical tree and quantiles); low-count full-resolution (n < k → no merging); rank monotonicity; skewed-distribution accuracy; config / value / count / `q` validation + `QDigestError.detail`; stats / reset / reconfigure; 8-thread concurrent adds; all 5 endpoints over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 106 — Complete.** All 229 test modules green. Sovereign Moment Sketch (Gan, Ding, Tai, Sheng, Bailis & Madden, 2018) — a **mergeable quantile sketch** that summarises a stream by its first `k` *power-sum moments* `C[i] = Σ xⁱ` (`i = 0..k-1`) together with the observed `min` / `max`. Quantiles are reconstructed at query time by fitting a **maximum-entropy (MaxEnt)** distribution to the moments: among all densities on `[min, max]` whose moments match the observed ones, the maximum-entropy choice is `p(x) ∝ exp(Σⱼ λⱼ·xʲ)`, with the values rescaled to the Chebyshev domain `[-1, 1]` for conditioning and the Lagrange multipliers `λ` solved by minimising the convex dual potential `log ∫ exp(Σⱼ λⱼ xʲ) dx − Σⱼ λⱼ μⱼ` (gradient = fitted − empirical moment) via `scipy.optimize.minimize` (L-BFGS-B). `quantile(q)` integrates the fitted density to a CDF and inverts it to find `v` with `CDF(v) = q`. Power sums are **trivially mergeable** — element-wise addition plus `min`/`max` of bounds — so distributed partitions combine in constant time. Fully deterministic (no randomness; `seed` carried for API parity). *(Collision note: the directive's originally-eyed **KLL Sketch is already shipped at Phase 92** — `class KLLSketch`, `pradyos/core/kll_sketch.py`, `/api/v1/kll` — so `kll_sketch` / `KLLSketch` read non-zero and were not reused; Phase 106 ships Moment Sketch instead.)* Depends on `numpy` / `scipy` (declared in `pyproject.toml`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/moment_sketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 106A: `pradyos/core/moment_sketch.py` — `MomentSketchError(detail)`; `MomentSketch(k=15, seed=0)` with `add(x)` (updates each power sum + min/max), `add_many(values)`, `quantile(q)` (`q` strictly in (0,1); MaxEnt fit; `MomentSketchError` on empty / bad `q`), `merge(other)` (same-`k` element-wise add + min/max; returns self; does not mutate `other`), `merge_state(dict)` / `from_state(dict)` (serialized-state round-trip), `reset(k=None, seed=None)`, `__len__` (= C[0]), `k`/`seed`/`total_count` properties, and `stats()` (k / seed / total_count / min_val / max_val / moments). Invalid `k`/`seed`, non-numeric value, or mismatched-`k` merge raise `MomentSketchError`.
- ✅ 106B: `pradyos/web/moment_sketch_web.py` — `register_momentsketch_routes(app, sketch=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/momentsketch/add` (body `{value}`; 422 on missing / non-numeric value), `GET /api/v1/momentsketch/quantile` (`?q=` with `Query(gt=0.0, lt=1.0)`; **422 on empty sketch**), `POST /api/v1/momentsketch/merge` (body = a serialized `stats()` state with a `moments` list → reconstructs and merges), `GET /api/v1/momentsketch/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/momentsketch/reset` (body `{k?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ✅ 106C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase106.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `moment_sketch` param, and a single `register_momentsketch_routes(app, moment_sketch)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 106D: `tests/test_moment_sketch.py` (61) + `tests/test_moment_sketch_web.py` (23) — **uniform p50** (10 000 values over [0,1000) → p50 ∈ [475,525]); **tail p99** within 5 % of 990; **merge correctness** (two 5 000-value complementary halves → merged p50 within 5 % of true); **strict monotonicity** of `quantile(0.25..0.99)`; **determinism** (same values + order → identical power sums and quantiles); **moment consistency** (C[0] = exact count; C[1]/C[0] = sample mean within 1 %; power sums match `Σxⁱ` by definition); skewed-exponential accuracy; quantile within `[min, max]`; merge element-wise add + min/max bounds + serialized-state round-trip + mismatched-`k` → error; config / value / `q` validation + `MomentSketchError.detail`; stats / reset / reconfigure; 8-thread concurrent adds; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. `DELETE`-with-body reset + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 107 — Complete.** All 231 test modules green. Sovereign Counting Bloom Filter — a Bloom variant whose single-bit array is replaced by an array of small integer **counters**, which buys the one thing a classic Bloom cannot do: **deletion**. `add` increments each of an element's `k` hashed counters; `remove` decrements them (guarded by a membership check first, so an absent element raises rather than under-decrementing and corrupting genuine members' counts); `contains` reports membership when *every* hashed counter is `≥ 1`. Standard Bloom sizing — `m = ⌈-n·ln(p)/(ln2)²⌉` counters and `k = ⌈(m/n)·ln2⌉` hash functions for capacity `n` and target error_rate `p`. Counters are **4-bit-valued** (16 states `0..15`, one byte each in an `array.array('B')`) and `add` **saturates** at 15, so a hot element can never overflow and corrupt the structure (the bounded cost: exact deletion is lost only for an element added more than 15 times). Hashing is a **double-hashing** scheme `h_i(x) = (h1(x) + i·h2(x)) mod m` for `i = 0..k-1`, where `h1`/`h2` are the two halves of one seeded BLAKE2b digest (the same stable, process-independent folding idiom as MinHash P88). Like any Bloom it admits **false positives** (bounded by `error_rate`) but — saturation aside — **no false negatives**. Pure stdlib (`array` + `hashlib`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/counting_bloom_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 107A: `pradyos/core/counting_bloom.py` — `CountingBloomError(detail)`; `CountingBloom(capacity=10000, error_rate=0.01, seed=0)` with `add(element)` (saturating increment), `contains(element)` / `__contains__`, `remove(element)` (decrement; raises `CountingBloomError("element not in filter")` if absent), `false_positive_rate()` (= `(1 - e^(-k·n/m))^k`), `reset(capacity=None, error_rate=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `capacity`/`error_rate`/`seed`/`num_hash_functions`/`num_counters`/`count` properties (`count` = number of `add` calls, *not* unique elements — noted in the docstring), and `stats()` (capacity / error_rate / num_hash_functions / num_counters / count / false_positive_rate). Invalid `capacity` (∉ ℤ⁺), `error_rate` (∉ (0,1)) or `seed` raise `CountingBloomError`.
- ✅ 107B: `pradyos/web/counting_bloom_web.py` — `register_countingbloom_routes(app, counting_bloom=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app filter) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/countingbloom/add` (body `{element}`; 422 on missing element), `GET /api/v1/countingbloom/contains` (`?element=`), `POST /api/v1/countingbloom/remove` (body `{element}`; **400 when the element is absent** — a state error, distinct from a 422 validation error), `GET /api/v1/countingbloom/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/countingbloom/reset` (body `{capacity?, error_rate?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ✅ 107C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase107.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `counting_bloom` param, and a single `register_countingbloom_routes(app, counting_bloom)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 107D: `tests/test_counting_bloom.py` (51) + `tests/test_countingbloom_web.py` (20) — **FPR accuracy** (1 000 members, 10 000 non-member probes → measured FPR ≤ 0.02); **no false negatives** (all 1 000 members contained); **deletion** (add → contains → remove → not contains); **double-add/single-remove** still present, **double-remove** gone; **no under-decrement corruption** (removing one element leaves 200 neighbours intact); **saturation** (add ×20 → counter capped at 15, no crash, still contained); **remove-of-absent raises** `CountingBloomError`; standard Bloom sizing (`m`/`k` formulae; tighter error_rate grows `m`); FPR formula + grows-with-load + zero-when-empty; determinism (same seed → identical counter array; survives reset; insertion-order independent; different seed → different array); config validation + `CountingBloomError.detail`; stats / reset / reconfigure; 8-thread concurrent adds; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. `DELETE`-with-body reset + the absent-remove **400** + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 108 — Complete.** All 233 test modules green. Sovereign Binary Fuse Filter (Graf & Lemire, 2022 — the segmented refinement of the fuse-graph construction, Dietzfelbinger & Walzer). Like the Phase 100 XOR filter it is a **static, space-optimal** approximate-membership filter built once from a complete key set; a query XORs three 8-bit fingerprint slots and compares against the key's own fingerprint, so there are **zero false negatives** and a false-positive rate of `≈ 2**-8 = 1/256 ≈ 0.39 %`. Hashing is a single seeded **xxhash-style** 64-bit integer mix — `mix(x, seed) = ((x ^ seed) · 0x517cc1b727220a95) & MASK64` (pure Python, no external dependency) — sliced into three segment-local indices `h_i = (mix >> 21·i) % segment` and a fingerprint `f = mix & 0xFF`; the three probed slots live in consecutive segments (`array[h0]`, `array[h1+seg]`, `array[h2+2·seg]`). Construction **peels** the 3-XOR hypergraph (repeatedly removing a slot touched by exactly one unassigned key) then assigns fingerprints in reverse peel order so each key's equation holds; peeling is probabilistic, so a stall triggers an **internal seed retry** (the seed is advanced deterministically, so a fixed key set still yields a reproducible filter). The filter is **immutable after build** — there is no incremental `add`; `reset` returns it to the unbuilt state. Keys are sorted internally, so build order does not change the result. Pure stdlib (`hashlib` + integer mixing); thread-safe via a single `threading.RLock` (build and contains can race). Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/binary_fuse_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 108A: `pradyos/core/binary_fuse.py` — `BinaryFuseError(detail)`; `BinaryFuseFilter(seed=0)` with `build(keys)` (static; sorts + dedups; `BinaryFuseError("duplicate keys")` on dups, `BinaryFuseError("build failed: cycle detected")` if peeling never converges across the internal seed retries), `contains(key)` / `__contains__` (`BinaryFuseError("filter not built")` before build), `reset(seed=None)` (back to unbuilt), `__len__`, `seed`/`built`/`array_size` properties, and `stats()` (built / num_keys / array_size / bits_per_key = `8·m/n` when built and non-empty else None / seed). Segments are sized at `⌈1.23·n/3⌉ + 4` slots each (`m = 3·segment`, ≈ 9.9 bits/key) — the regime where 3-segment peeling is reliable.
- ✅ 108B: `pradyos/web/binary_fuse_web.py` — `register_binaryfuse_routes(app, binary_fuse=None)` (defaults to a fresh unbuilt filter) mounts 4 (all-static) routes — **no insert (the filter is static)**: `POST /api/v1/binaryfuse/build` (body `{keys: [...]}`; 422 on missing / non-list keys, **400** on duplicate / build cycle), `GET /api/v1/binaryfuse/contains` (`?key=`; **400 before build**), `GET /api/v1/binaryfuse/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/binaryfuse/reset` (body `{seed?}`; 422 on bad seed).
- ✅ 108C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase108.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `binary_fuse` param, and a single `register_binaryfuse_routes(app, binary_fuse)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 108D: `tests/test_binary_fuse.py` (49) + `tests/test_binaryfuse_web.py` (20) — **no false negatives** (every built key contained, small and large key sets); **FPR** ≤ 0.005 over 10 000 non-member probes (≈ 1/256 theory); **space efficiency** (`bits_per_key ≤ 10`, `array_size ≈ 1.23·n + 12`); **determinism** (same seed + keys → identical array, survives retries) + **order-independence** (`build([a,b,c]) == build([c,a,b])`, incl. large reversed sets) + different-seed → different array; **immutability** (no `add`; rebuild replaces); duplicate-keys / not-built / cycle → `BinaryFuseError`; build across sizes `n = 1..3000`; reset → unbuilt + contains raises + rebuildable; 8-thread concurrent `contains`; all 4 endpoints over HTTP incl. `DELETE`-with-body reset, the build-duplicate **400**, the contains-before-build **400**, + a prior-phase regression check.
- ✅ 108E: `scripts/prove.py` — 233 test modules registered (Phase 108 appends `test_binary_fuse.py` + `test_binaryfuse_web.py`).

**Phase 109 — Complete.** All 235 test modules green. Sovereign Vacuum Filter (Wang, Zhou, Yang, Du, Yang & Uhlig, 2019) — a space-efficient approximate-membership filter in the **cuckoo-fingerprint** family (cf. the Phase 86 cuckoo filter) supporting both **insertion** and **deletion** while using *less* space than the cuckoo filter at the same false-positive rate. The cuckoo filter recovers an item's alternate bucket by `i2 = i1 XOR H(fp)`, which is an involution over `[0, m)` **only when the bucket count `m` is rounded up to a power of two** — wasting on average ~1.5× (up to 2×) the space actually needed. The Vacuum Filter removes that constraint with an **Alternate Range** `L` (a power of two): both candidate buckets are confined to the same `L`-aligned *chunk* of `L` consecutive buckets via `i2 = i1 XOR (H(fp) mod L)`. Because `H(fp) mod L < L` flips only the low `log2(L)` bits, `i1` and `i2` always share the chunk `[⌊i1/L⌋·L, ⌊i1/L⌋·L + L)`; the bucket count then only has to be a **multiple of `L`** (`m = num_chunks · L`) rather than a power of two, so it sits much closer to the true required size (measured **18–44 % smaller** than the cuckoo filter's next-power-of-two across n = 1.1k–100k). Each chunk is an independent power-of-two cuckoo sub-table, so intra-chunk partial-key kicking reaches high occupancy (**≈ 0.95 load** at first insert failure, measured) while the chunk count absorbs the rest at fine granularity. The XOR stays an involution because `⌊i1/L⌋·L` is a multiple of `L` (low bits zero) and `m` is a multiple of `L` (so `chunk_base + L ≤ m`), and the displacement depends only on the fingerprint — so a kicked fingerprint **never leaves its origin chunk** and the filter **never reports a false negative** (a failed insert is rolled back atomically), while `contains` may false-positive at `≈ 2·bucket_size / 2^fingerprint_bits` exactly as the cuckoo filter does. The hash is injectable (`hash_fn`) for deterministic tests, with a `seed` salting the default stable BLAKE2b fold (process-independent). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock` (the public surface acquires it; internal helpers under the lock never re-acquire it). Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/vacuum_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 109A: `pradyos/core/vacuum_filter.py` — `VacuumFilterError(detail)`; `VacuumFilter(capacity, bucket_size=4, fingerprint_bits=8, max_kicks=500, alt_range=None, seed=0, hash_fn=None)` with `insert(item)` (partial-key cuckoo kicking confined to the item's chunk; atomic rollback → returns `False` when the chunk is full), `contains(item)` / `__contains__`, `delete(item)` (removes one fingerprint; `False` if absent), `reset()`, `__len__`, and `capacity` (bucket count = `num_chunks·alt_range`) / `alt_range` / `num_chunks` / `seed` properties, plus `stats()` (capacity / num_chunks / alt_range / count / load_factor / fingerprint_bits / max_kicks). `alt_range` defaults to an auto-chosen power of two (~8 large chunks) and is validated as a power of two (and clamped to fit `capacity`); invalid `capacity` / `bucket_size` / `fingerprint_bits` (>32) / `max_kicks` / `seed` / `alt_range` raise `VacuumFilterError` (bools rejected).
- ✅ 109B: `pradyos/web/vacuum_web.py` — `register_vacuum_routes(app, vacuum_filter=None)` (defaults to a fresh `VacuumFilter` cap 1024) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/vacuum/insert` (body `{item}`; 422 on missing / non-dict body), `POST /api/v1/vacuum/contains` (body `{item}`; 422 on missing), `DELETE /api/v1/vacuum/delete` (body `{item}`; 422 on missing), `GET /api/v1/vacuum/stats`, `POST /api/v1/vacuum/reset`.
- ✅ 109C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase109.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `vacuum_filter` param, and a single `register_vacuum_routes(app, vacuum_filter)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 109D: `tests/test_vacuum_filter.py` (61) + `tests/test_vacuum_web.py` (20) — **no false negatives** (every inserted key contained, small sets and high-occupancy fills); **involution + chunk confinement** (`alt(alt(i,fp),fp)==i`, `i1`/`i2` share the `L`-aligned chunk, both in `[0,m)` over thousands of keys); **space efficiency** (`m` a multiple of `alt_range`, `m == num_chunks·alt_range`, `m ≤ next_pow2(capacity)` at every size and strictly `<` for non-power-of-two chunk counts — `cap=3000 → m=3072 < 4096`); **high occupancy** (≥ 0.90 load before first failure, zero false negatives); **FPR** (default hash, 8-bit fp, `b=4` → measured ≤ 0.05 over the ~3.1 % theory) + **wider fingerprint** (16-bit → ≤ 0.005); **deletion** (insert → contains → delete → absent; reinsert; injected-collision false-positive clears on delete); **determinism** (injected hash and same-`seed` reproducible; different `seed` diverges placement); auto/explicit `alt_range` layout (`cap=3000 → L=256, 12 chunks`; `cap=4096 → L=512, 8 chunks`); full-chunk rollback (no corruption, count unchanged); config validation + `VacuumFilterError.detail`; stats / reset / reset-preserves-layout; 10-thread concurrent inserts + concurrent insert/delete; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. `DELETE`-with-body delete + deterministic FP-and-clear + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `binaryfuse`).
- ✅ 109E: `scripts/prove.py` — 235 test modules registered (Phase 109 appends `test_vacuum_filter.py` + `test_vacuum_web.py`).
- ✅ 109F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 110 planned.

**Phase 110 — Complete.** All 237 test modules green. Sovereign Stable Bloom Filter (Deng & Rafiei, SIGMOD 2006) — a Bloom variant for **unbounded data streams**. A classic Bloom (Phase 72) or Counting Bloom (Phase 107) **saturates** on an endless stream: every cell eventually fills, the false-positive rate climbs to 1, and the filter is useless. The Stable Bloom Filter fixes this by **continuously forgetting** — it stores an array of small `d`-bit **cells** (each in `0..Max`, `Max = 2^d − 1`) and on *every* insertion first **decrements `P` uniformly-random cells** (floored at 0) before **setting the element's `k` hashed cells to `Max`**. The decrement step evicts stale information at a constant rate, so the count of zero cells converges to a non-zero steady state regardless of stream length — the fill ratio (and hence the FP rate) **stabilises** instead of growing (measured: fill plateaus at **~0.58** across 5k→120k inserts, never saturating). `contains` reports membership when every one of an element's `k` cells is `≥ 1`; because a set cell can later be decremented to 0, the filter admits a small **bounded false-negative** rate for *old* elements (recent inserts recalled with ~1.0 probability; stale items measured ~0.87 forgotten after flooding) — the deliberate price for bounded memory on an infinite stream, and exactly what separates it from the no-false-negative Bloom family. `P` defaults to `num_hashes · max_value` (the balance point where mass removed ≈ mass added), tunable for a tighter FP/FN trade (Deng & Rafiei derive the optimal `P` from a target stable FP). Cells are one byte each in an `array.array('B')` (`Max ≤ 255`); hashing is double-hashing `h_i = (h1 + i·h2) mod m` from one seeded BLAKE2b digest (the MinHash/Counting-Bloom idiom); the eviction draws from a `random.Random(seed)` so a fixed seed + insertion sequence reproduce the filter exactly. Pure stdlib (`array` + `hashlib` + `random`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/stable_bloom_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ✅ 110A: `pradyos/core/stable_bloom.py` — `StableBloomError(detail)`; `StableBloomFilter(num_cells=10000, num_hashes=5, max_value=3, decrement=None, seed=0)` with `add(element)` (evict `P` random cells then set `k` cells to `Max`), `contains(element)` / `__contains__`, `fill_ratio()` (fraction of non-zero cells), `reset(...)` (clear / reconfigure; re-seeds the eviction RNG), `__len__`, and `num_cells` / `num_hashes` / `max_value` / `decrement` (P) / `seed` / `count` properties, plus `stats()` (num_cells / num_hashes / max_value / decrement / count / fill_ratio / seed). `decrement` defaults to `min(num_hashes·max_value, num_cells)`; invalid `num_cells` / `num_hashes` / `max_value` (∉ 1..255) / `decrement` (∉ 1..num_cells) / `seed` raise `StableBloomError` (bools rejected).
- ✅ 110B: `pradyos/web/stable_bloom_web.py` — `register_stablebloom_routes(app, stable_bloom=None)` (defaults to a fresh `StableBloomFilter`) mounts 4 (all-static) routes — **no remove (the filter forgets on its own)**: `POST /api/v1/stablebloom/add` (body `{element}`; 422 on missing / non-dict), `GET /api/v1/stablebloom/contains` (`?element=`), `GET /api/v1/stablebloom/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/stablebloom/reset` (body `{num_cells?, num_hashes?, max_value?, decrement?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ✅ 110C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase110.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `stable_bloom` param, and a single `register_stablebloom_routes(app, stable_bloom)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ✅ 110D: `tests/test_stable_bloom.py` (43) + `tests/test_stablebloom_web.py` (18) — **fresh add recalled**; **empty contains → False**; **stability** (fill plateaus over a 40k stream, never `≥ 0.95`); **recent recall** (`≥ 0.95`); **forgetting** (stale victims evicted after flooding, FN_old `≥ 0.5`); **FP bounded** (`< 0.20` after warmup); **no saturation** under heavy stream; **larger `max_value` ⇒ higher recall**; **determinism** (same seed + sequence → identical stats & membership; different seed diverges; reset re-seeds the RNG); default/explicit `decrement` (k·Max, capped at num_cells); config validation + `StableBloomError.detail` (incl. `max_value > 255`, `decrement > num_cells`, bools); stats / properties / fill_ratio; reset clears + reconfigures; 10-thread concurrent adds + concurrent add/contains; all 4 endpoints over HTTP incl. `DELETE`-with-body reset + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `vacuum`).
